LEXICON Verb

! contlex stem umlaut dict class
! ------------------------------------
! BÅETEDH_TV even row A class I
! ÅARAJEHTEDH even row A class I derived words -ehtedh, -estedh, -iste SOVVEDH ;
! GÅETEDH even row A class I derived words -gåete SOVVEDH ;
! ÅEREDH  even row A class I
! TJEARODH even row C class II
! TSEAHKODH even row C class II
! GUARKEDH_TV even row B class III
! TJOEHPEDH_TV even row D class IV
! GOEGKERDADTEDH even row D class IV derived words -alledh, -adte SOVVEDH ;
! SOVVEDH even row D class IV derived words -sovvedh, htalledh = passives
! AHTJE ! row D class IV derived words -ahtje
! BÅÅHKEDH even row E class V
! VÅÅJNEDH even row E class V
! GÖÖLEDH even row F class VI
! GOLTELIDH odd !odd-syll with -adte- as Der2
! DÅAJVOEHTIDH odd !for stems ending -t-: dåajvoeht-, odd-syll with -alle- as Der2
! LGIDH odd ending -lgi SOVVEDH ;
! ------------------------------------
! Auxiliaries
! NEG
! LEA
! EDTJEDH

! First auxiliaries, then some irregular stray forms, 
! and then the full lexicon, ordered mainly by stem type
! (but the end of the doc has some lists). At some
! point we will alphabetise this file.

! Auxiliaries
! ===========

ij+V+Neg: NEG ;
lea+V: LEA ;
edtjedh+V:edtj EDTJEDH ;
